<name>Brian Hodge< /name><time>1620618199597< /time><Rate>1</Rate>< Text>
My van had its check engine light come on in May of 2020. I took it to T&M to have them look at it. They stated they would check the code, and get back to me as soon as they could. They had a high number of cars to work on, so I understood it might take a while to get to my van.

Come July, and I had not heard from them yet, so I called to see what is going on, and they said they would call me back. Still nothing for a while, and I was getting worried. It is now September, and still nothing. October comes, and I get a hold of them, and they tell me a needed a new engine.

This was ridiculous because I had just put a new engine in my van through T&M just over a year ago, and it should have been under warranty. Eventually, I called them again saying that I just put in an engine with them, and it should still be under warranty. I talked to the owner, Jorge Fajardo, about it, and he agreed to not charge for the engine since it was warranty, though later he stated that the warranty was expired, but still did not charge me since they were the last ones to put in the engine previously.

So, they go to "work" on the engine, and come November, they were going to get a new engine again because the one they ordered "did not work." My car was "finished" in December, and I finally took it home. Jorge said he would mail me the paperwork for the work, though I never did receive it.

At the advice of my father, I took my van over to my friend who is a retired mechanic to do a couple of checks on it. When he looked at it, he discovered that the engine in my car was the original one I put in with T&M over a year ago, and he stated they did not do a single thing to my car, as some of the codes that were an issue originally when I put it in to T&M were still popping up. My mechanic friend fixed the parts of the car that caused the codes to pop up, and still had to do some addition maintenance after the fact. Currently, it is running pretty well, thanks to my mechanic friend, and not T&M Automotive.

I am very disappointed in T&M Automotive. My van sat in their shop for almost 1/2 of a year, and they did nothing to repair my car, but were wanting to charge me for a new engine that my car did not need. That is probably why I never received the paperwork on the repair; because they did nothing to fix the van.

T&M in the past were great with their repairs and maintenance, and at a very efficient rate and time. Now, I cannot in good conscience recommend them to anyone after this experience. I feel as though they were trying to get a quick buck from me by saying I needed a new engine, despite the fact that they put one in recently for me, and when I said that I would not be paying for a new engine I thought was still under warranty, they stringed me along until they said they "Fixed my van" when nothing was done.

I stand by this statement: Do not go to T&M Automotive.< /Text>

<userid>109744811928433206378</userid><Name>Amy Palmer< /Name>< Time>

<rate>4</rate>< review>
3/28/15

I've seen Dr. Zimmerman in this office twice and both times the office was running on schedule - or at least less than 15 minutes behind schedule, which is good enough for me. I usually call ahead to make sure I don't show up for appointments and then sit in a waiting room for an hour, but some places have front desk staff that just refuse to admit the doctor is 30 minutes behind! Not here.

The waiting room is clean and nice and had little samples of sensitive skin Dove soap available last time I went in.

The BEST thing about this office is being able to email to request an appointment. I went to their website, explained what I wanted checked out, and had an email response the next day when I was at work. I didn't have to take a personal call at their convenience, but was able to request a date and respond to their emails when I had a break - totally convenient! The appointment wasn't that far out either.

You don't have to have skin issues to need a visit to a dermatologist. They do cancer screenings, which is important for everyone! My cousin died of melanoma last year and he was only in his 30s, so naturally I'm concerned about every spot I see - it's nice to be reassured that I'm just being paranoid.  Never ever wait to check out something on your body that concerns you. They also offer cosmetic treatments, facials, and skin products of all types, so hopefully my next visit will be for one of these services.</review>

If you‚Äôre looking for someone with a good attitude and prompt customer service your search ends here. For my C-class family out there my ESL failed in the locked position at 69K. When the ESL fails in the locked position it can no longer correlate with the EIS and the car refuses to start. Rebuilding the ESL would‚Äôve taken 2-3 weeks to receive components; not to mention it would only be a matter of time before the China components failed again. Quickest most feasible solution was an ELV aka emulator which completely replaces and mimics the ELS. < review>
I stopped by for a quick take out breakfast burrito.  I was pleasantly greeted and decided to eat in.  In the morning they serve you a fresh, hot sopapilla, with honey at the table, yum!    I really like that they offer whole black beans as an alternative to pinto; a healthier choice for me.  All food made fresh to order.  They have fresh hot sauces of varying degrees and taste, including green tomatillo.  Service is friendly and inviting.  Decor is simple and casual.  Comfortable seating for one, two, groups, etc.   Clean, tidy, and open floor plan.  For breakfast, lunch, and dinner.  Some selections of beer and wine. Happy hour 3-6pm, Monday thru Friday.  They also offer catering and full pot take out of Menudo.  I would cerainly recommend this place.</review>

<username>Jasmine Hoover<//username>< Date>
1543511883622< /Date>
< Rate>
5<//Rate>
<text>Love this place. My family is from New Mexico and this is almost the only place around to get pretty authentic New Mexico cuisine, so we go as a family for anniversaries and stuff. The prices are good, about $8-12 a plate. This is not traditional Mexican food or Tex-Mex, it's pretty New Mexico specific, which means it smacks of Mexican food but with a spin, lots of fried dough and dishes centered around red and green chiles. If you've never had New Mexican food, definitely get the stuffed sopapilla, which is the classic, and get it smothered.  It's fried dough stuffed with beans and green or red chile and meat, topped in red or green chile, cream and cheese.  ALWAYS get an order of plain sopapillas with honey for dessert.  The green chile soup is actually fantastic too and the New Mexico style enchilada stack with an egg on top is prob my second choice as far as main dishes.  If you're New Mexican, of course, this won't live up to the real deal, mainly that the spice levels are way toned down for Californians, but you can usually get it still spicy enough to enjoy it.  The service is unfortunately almost always pretty nonattentive, but it's a really great casual, inexpensive place to go as a family with really tasty food< /text>< Pictures>
None</Pictures>

<review>Bellanico was a nice sit-down restaurant with a great feel, ambiance, and experience.

I stumbled upon this place on a recommendation and went with a few people.  We noticed there was a prefix menu for the night.. so that was a good way to try many of their offerings!

Our first dish we got was toast with cured salmon paste on it.  The toast was crispy and had a nice texture to it.  The paste was a good accompaniment and it was a nice dish to munch on.  We then were able to try the wild boar and ricotta ravioli.  I liked the ravioli though it was a pretty plain dish and did not think anything much of it.

I was also able to get the Russet potato gnocchi with gargonzola cream and toasted almonds.  This was my favorite dish here.  The almonds provide a nice texture and the gnocchi was prepared well and tasted great.

For dessert I got the goat cheese cheesecake.  This was a nice tasting cheesecake and it was not overly sweet.  It just had the right amount of minimal sweetness which I liked.

I really like the interior of this restaurant and the service was very attentive and nice.  I definitely would come back!<//review>< rating>

<Date>1485322975624<//Date><Rate>4<//Rate><Review>Other than the noise and extreme busy-ness that made it hard to have a nice , enjoyable dinner, it was very good.  I didn't realize it was Oakland Restaurant Week so perhaps that explains it.; but tables are very close together which made it worse.
However the food and service were great.  The duck pate was wonderful, the milk-braised pork shoulder on pasta was a great blend of flavors and cooked to perfection.  My partner had the meatball appetizer which was fair, and the Gnocchi with mushrooms which was very flavorful.
We had the Venetian donuts for dessert which were interesting and fine but I wouldn't order them again.  Wine selection was nice.  Our server was very personable and welcoming and provided great service throughout the entire meal.
Lastly, we very much appreciated the choice of two sizes for the entrees; that is perfect for us and I wish more restaurants offered this option.  Aside from allowing us to leave room for dessert, it's nice on the budget as well.  I recommend the restaurant and look forward to our next visit.< /Review>< Pics>

<user>118109329288882500468< /user><name>de ann freitag< /name><Date>1536693485381< /Date>< Rate>
4< /Rate>
< text>
Was invited to dinner there last Saturday night.  While the food was good, the execution left a lot to be desired.  Did not get bread for 50 minutes after sitting down.  Duck pate appetizer order was totally forgotten; it ended up being served with the Primo course once waiter was reminded it was a dish we ordered.  The pate was dense, creamy and had lovely flavor.  Fried Squash Blossoms with lentils were fabulous.  The panna cotta, pork belly, and farro salad dishes were enjoyed by the others.  Two diners had the Liberty duck breast/leg - breast was moist and tender; leg was a little dry.  The risotto was tasty with pine nuts and the pork chop was huge - she took half of it home.  But nicely cooked.  The waiter was a bit testy about us bringing our own Amarone wine to share but this varietal was not on their menu.  A lecture about how we should put the $20 corkage fee towards buying one of their bottles of wine is not really the way customers should be treated.  Still, it could have just been an off night for our server and we should try again.  But parking in the area is really awful.    So realistically, we probably will not return.< /text>

The restaurant was practically empty, with only one customer ahead of my coworker and myself. We both ordered salads. I placed my order first. It took 30 minutes for my coworker to get her salad order, which was placed several minutes after mine (I ordered a Southwest Chicken Salad). There were at least 5 people working in the kitchen. I really can't say what they were working on, but it most certainly was not my simple salad! After being asked 3 times, what I ordered, I simply decided to get my refund! No apology for poor service, no anything! All I heard as I was leaving,  was "cancel the salad!" Since when does it take more than 30 minutes to make a salad?! I will not return! Zero stars if it was possible!<//Review>

< user_name>
Eric Miller<//user_name>
< text>
First time to eat at The Habit today. A friend recommended it to me because he knows I love cheese burgers. The first thing I noticed when we walked in was the temperature in the restaurant, warm. If the A/C was on it was set pretty high. Very stuffy stagnate air in the dinning area. Was greated by a friendly women who I assumed was a manager or shift leader because she was wearing a different colored shirt than everyone else. I ordered the sesonal item, Santa Barbara Char burger. Comes with 2 burger patties both topped with cheddar cheese and grilled onions, lettuce, tomatoes, pickles and avocado. I also got an order of fries, well done,  because lets be honest, fries are never as crispy as they should be because restaurants are in such a hurry to get food out. Also ordered the tempura green beans. My friend got the single char with swiss, grilled onions and lettuce. He's kind of a plain guy, I always say you can tell a lot about a person by how they order a cheese burger. Anywho my Santa Barbara burger was good the patties were seasoned properly the cheese was perfectly gooey, melty, the grilled onions were ok. Not as carmelized as they could be in my opinion. The Santa Barbara char comes on grilled bread not your traditional hamburger bun. All in all a pretty good burger. It just still has that synthetic fast food feel about it. No home made love feel like I get at In n Out or Riders Club. The fries were cooked well as I ordered them but you could tell they were frozen. Definitely not In n Out fresh cut quality. The tempura green beans were good. But for $2.99 I feel like we should have got more than what they gave us, kinda stingy if you know what I mean. Drink selection was good. I'm an iced tea guy so it was pretty cool they had three fresh brewed teas to choose from, black tea, tropical tea and a citrus green tea. Also had strawberry limeade which was pretty good. In the end I would eat here again if I was in the area and didn't want to wait the 15 minutes it would take to get to In n Out.</text>

< Review>
I came here to get my son his birthday charburger.
While I was there I placed an order for my other sons and a burger for myself.
I placed the order to go because I didn't want to spend too much time in a crowded place with everything that has been going on.
I don't exactly live near this location, it's a good 10 miles or so from home.
I got notification that my order was ready.
The person working stated that the burgers were in one bag, underneath the fries and the other bag contained the kid's meal for my little one.
I looked inside and saw the burgers under there so I assumed they were all there.
When I got home and opened the bag, I immediately noticed that there was a burger missing, my burger.
The one that I paid extra for.
Their promotional Jalopeno Tempura Charburger.
I am usually a calm person, but I can not stand people who do not do their job properly.
This person stated to me that the burgers were under the fries.
Obviously, he was wrong.
I felt ripped off.
I paid for something that I did not receive.
I tried to call the store but calling the number does not result in contacting anyone physically at the location, but rather a call center.
Completely POINTLESS!
I am not going to drive 20-25 minutes go get something I was supposed to have in the first place.
When someone places an order, especially when it's to go, there should be extra care taken to make sure everything is in order.
There is nothing that can be done now to fix what has happened.
You guys dropped the ball here.
This is totally unacceptable and I do not see myself returning to this location again.</Review>

<Text>First time to eat at The Habit today. A friend recommended it to me because he knows I love cheese burgers. The first thing I noticed when we walked in was the temperature in the restaurant, warm. If the A/C was on it was set pretty high. Very stuffy stagnate air in the dinning area. Was greated by a friendly women who I assumed was a manager or shift leader because she was wearing a different colored shirt than everyone else. I ordered the sesonal item, Santa Barbara Char burger. Comes with 2 burger patties both topped with cheddar cheese and grilled onions, lettuce, tomatoes, pickles and avocado. I also got an order of fries, well done,  because lets be honest, fries are never as crispy as they should be because restaurants are in such a hurry to get food out. Also ordered the tempura green beans. My friend got the single char with swiss, grilled onions and lettuce. He's kind of a plain guy, I always say you can tell a lot about a person by how they order a cheese burger. Anywho my Santa Barbara burger was good the patties were seasoned properly the cheese was perfectly gooey, melty, the grilled onions were ok. Not as carmelized as they could be in my opinion. The Santa Barbara char comes on grilled bread not your traditional hamburger bun. All in all a pretty good burger. It just still has that synthetic fast food feel about it. No home made love feel like I get at In n Out or Riders Club. The fries were cooked well as I ordered them but you could tell they were frozen. Definitely not In n Out fresh cut quality. The tempura green beans were good. But for $2.99 I feel like we should have got more than what they gave us, kinda stingy if you know what I mean. Drink selection was good. I'm an iced tea guy so it was pretty cool they had three fresh brewed teas to choose from, black tea, tropical tea and a citrus green tea. Also had strawberry limeade which was pretty good. In the end I would eat here again if I was in the area and didn't want to wait the 15 minutes it would take to get to In n Out.< /Text>< time>

< text>
This is my first time and also last, went there at 5pm today,  the line was long, took 10 minutes to order then waited 15 minutes to get my food. Meat patties were dry and tasteless. I ordered the mushrooms char, the golden chicken sandwich, and also 2 of Santa Barbara style as well. Thought trying more than one thing would be great but they were all terrible. My buns were chewy and very dry like they are old, pretty nasty. I threw most of my food away including the fries, very bland. I ordered tempura green beans and they were not crunchy but at least it was not bland. I asked for no pickles, spicy sauce for the chicken on the side, and avocado on the side because of food allergies. They ignored all request and that's why I'll never go back. They also give half patty on the Santa Barbara style instead of full meat patty... that was just a rip off. What I liked about this place... seating area outside.</text>
